^SERIES = GSE129800
!Series_title = Tumor- and cytokine-primed human natural killer cells exhibit distinct phenotypic and transcriptional signatures [Nanostring]
!Series_geo_accession = GSE129800
!Series_status = Public on Jun 12 2019
!Series_submission_date = Apr 15 2019
!Series_last_update_date = Sep 12 2019
!Series_pubmed_id = 31242243
!Series_summary = An emerging cellular immunotherapy for cancer is based on the cytolytic activity of natural killer (NK) cells against a wide range of tumors. Although in vitro activation or ‘priming’ of NK cells by exposure to pro-inflammatory cytokines such as interleukin (IL)-2 has been extensively studied, the biological consequences of NK cell activation in response to target cell interactions are less characterized. Herein, we investigate the consequences of co-incubation with K562, CTV-1, Daudi and RPMI-8226 tumor cell lines on the phenotype, cytokine expression profile and transcriptome of human NK cells. We observe the downregulation of several activation receptors including CD16, CD62L, C-X-C chemokine receptor (CXCR)-4, natural killer group 2 member D (NKG2D), DNAX accessory molecule (DNAM)-1 and NKp46 following tumor-priming. Although this NK cell phenotype is typically associated with NK cell dysfunction in cancer, we show upregulation of NK cell activation markers such as CD69 and CD25, secretion of pro-inflammatory cytokines including macrophage inflammatory proteins (MIP-1) α /β and IL-1β/6/8 and overexpression of numerous genes associated with enhanced NK cell cytotoxicity and immunomodulatory functions such as FAS, TNFSF10, MAPK11, TNF and IFNG.
!Series_summary = Key signaling molecules exclusively affected by tumor-priming include MAP2K3, MARCKSL1, STAT5A, and TNFAIP3, which are specifically associated with NK cell cytotoxicity against tumor targets. Collectively, these findings help define the phenotypic and transcriptional signature of NK cells following their encounter with tumor cells, independent of cytokine stimulation, and provide insight into tumor-specific NK cell responses to inform the transition towards harnessing the therapeutic potential of NK cells in cancer.  
!Series_overall_design = The mRNA profiles of freshly isolated healthy donor-derived human NK cells after stimulation with tumor cells (CTV-1) or cytokine (IL-2)  were analyzed and compared to unstimulated controls (NK alone).

^SAMPLE = GSM3722267
!Sample_title = NK alone donor 1
!Sample_geo_accession = GSM3722267
!Sample_status = Public on Jun 11 2019
!Sample_submission_date = Apr 15 2019
!Sample_last_update_date = Jun 11 2019
!Sample_type = RNA
!Sample_channel_count = 1
!Sample_source_name_ch1 = Control
!Sample_organism_ch1 = Homo sapiens
!Sample_taxid_ch1 = 9606
!Sample_characteristics_ch1 = tissue: peripheral blood
!Sample_characteristics_ch1 = cell type: natural killer cells
!Sample_treatment_protocol_ch1 = NK cell stimulation was achieved by co-incubating CD56+ NK cells (1x10^6) with CTV-1 (2x10^6) for 6 or 16 hours, or the exogenous cytokine IL-2 (200IU/ml) for  16 hours at 37ºC, 5% v/v CO2 in CM.
!Sample_growth_protocol_ch1 = NK cells were isolated from healthy donor PBMCs by positive selection for CD56 (CD56 MicroBeads; Miltenyi Biotec) according to the manufacturer’s instructions. Freshly isolated NK cells were maintained in complete medium (CM) (RPMI 1640 supplemented with 10% v/v fetal bovine serum and 2mM L-glutamine; all from Life Technologies). The  acute lymphoblastic leukemia cell line CTV-1 was maintained in CM.
!Sample_molecule_ch1 = polyA RNA
!Sample_extract_protocol_ch1 = To prepare the samples, resting NK cells (5x10^5) were washed twice and incubated alone or mixed with mitomycin-C-treated CTV-1 cells (1x10^6) for 6 hours, or IL-2 (200 IU/ml) for 16 hours at 37°C in 5% v/v CO2. Thereafter, NK cells were selectively enriched from co-culture by CD56 isolation, and RNA was extracted from the samples using the RNAqueousTM Micro Kit (Thermo Fisher Scientific).
!Sample_label_ch1 = Target-probe complex
!Sample_label_protocol_ch1 = Batches of 12 separate samples at one time were prepared as per manufacturer’s instructions.  Platform used was human myeloid innate immunity panel (Catalog number XT-CSO-HMMYLD1-12).
!Sample_hyb_protocol = Samples were hybridized with probes at 65°C for 18 hours before being placed into the automated nCounter™ Prep Station (NanoString Technologies), where samples were affixed to cartridges.
!Sample_scan_protocol = Cartridges were immediately placed into the nCounter™ Digital Analyzer (Nanostring Technologies) and read at maximum resolution
!Sample_description = Control
!Sample_data_processing = Using nSolver software, QC  was carried out using default QC parameter settings. Then, raw data files  were examined to ensure that counts of positive and negative controls as well as housekeeping/endogenous genes meet expectations. Thereafter, background noise was adjusted by background thresholding using a user-defined threshold count value of 20 counts. Normalization was accomplished using the geometric mean of the positive control counts, and housekeeping genes in the CodeSet Content. Differential expression was calculated by specifying NK alone samples as the baseline of the experiment using nSolver software.

!Sample_title = NK alone donor 2
!Sample_geo_accession = GSM3722268
!Sample_status = Public on Jun 11 2019
!Sample_submission_date = Apr 15 2019
!Sample_last_update_date = Jun 11 2019
!Sample_type = RNA
!Sample_channel_count = 1
!Sample_source_name_ch1 = Control
!Sample_organism_ch1 = Homo sapiens
!Sample_taxid_ch1 = 9606
!Sample_characteristics_ch1 = tissue: peripheral blood
!Sample_characteristics_ch1 = cell type: natural killer cells
!Sample_treatment_protocol_ch1 = NK cell stimulation was achieved by co-incubating CD56+ NK cells (1x10^6) with CTV-1 (2x10^6) for 6 or 16 hours, or the exogenous cytokine IL-2 (200IU/ml) for  16 hours at 37ºC, 5% v/v CO2 in CM.
!Sample_growth_protocol_ch1 = NK cells were isolated from healthy donor PBMCs by positive selection for CD56 (CD56 MicroBeads; Miltenyi Biotec) according to the manufacturer’s instructions. Freshly isolated NK cells were maintained in complete medium (CM) (RPMI 1640 supplemented with 10% v/v fetal bovine serum and 2mM L-glutamine; all from Life Technologies). The  acute lymphoblastic leukemia cell line CTV-1 was maintained in CM.
!Sample_molecule_ch1 = polyA RNA
!Sample_extract_protocol_ch1 = To prepare the samples, resting NK cells (5x10^5) were washed twice and incubated alone or mixed with mitomycin-C-treated CTV-1 cells (1x10^6) for 6 hours, or IL-2 (200 IU/ml) for 16 hours at 37°C in 5% v/v CO2. Thereafter, NK cells were selectively enriched from co-culture by CD56 isolation, and RNA was extracted from the samples using the RNAqueousTM Micro Kit (Thermo Fisher Scientific).
!Sample_label_ch1 = Target-probe complex
!Sample_label_protocol_ch1 = Batches of 12 separate samples at one time were prepared as per manufacturer’s instructions.  Platform used was human myeloid innate immunity panel (Catalog number XT-CSO-HMMYLD1-12).
!Sample_hyb_protocol = Samples were hybridized with probes at 65°C for 18 hours before being placed into the automated nCounter™ Prep Station (NanoString Technologies), where samples were affixed to cartridges.
!Sample_scan_protocol = Cartridges were immediately placed into the nCounter™ Digital Analyzer (Nanostring Technologies) and read at maximum resolution
!Sample_description = Control
!Sample_data_processing = Using nSolver software, QC  was carried out using default QC parameter settings. Then, raw data files  were examined to ensure that counts of positive and negative controls as well as housekeeping/endogenous genes meet expectations. Thereafter, background noise was adjusted by background thresholding using a user-defined threshold count value of 20 counts. Normalization was accomplished using the geometric mean of the positive control counts, and housekeeping genes in the CodeSet Content. Differential expression was calculated by specifying NK alone samples as the baseline of the experiment using nSolver software.

!Sample_title = NK alone donor 3
!Sample_geo_accession = GSM3722269
!Sample_status = Public on Jun 11 2019
!Sample_submission_date = Apr 15 2019
!Sample_last_update_date = Jun 11 2019
!Sample_type = RNA
!Sample_channel_count = 1
!Sample_source_name_ch1 = Control
!Sample_organism_ch1 = Homo sapiens
!Sample_taxid_ch1 = 9606
!Sample_characteristics_ch1 = tissue: peripheral blood
!Sample_characteristics_ch1 = cell type: natural killer cells
!Sample_treatment_protocol_ch1 = NK cell stimulation was achieved by co-incubating CD56+ NK cells (1x10^6) with CTV-1 (2x10^6) for 6 or 16 hours, or the exogenous cytokine IL-2 (200IU/ml) for  16 hours at 37ºC, 5% v/v CO2 in CM.
!Sample_growth_protocol_ch1 = NK cells were isolated from healthy donor PBMCs by positive selection for CD56 (CD56 MicroBeads; Miltenyi Biotec) according to the manufacturer’s instructions. Freshly isolated NK cells were maintained in complete medium (CM) (RPMI 1640 supplemented with 10% v/v fetal bovine serum and 2mM L-glutamine; all from Life Technologies). The  acute lymphoblastic leukemia cell line CTV-1 was maintained in CM.
!Sample_molecule_ch1 = polyA RNA
!Sample_extract_protocol_ch1 = To prepare the samples, resting NK cells (5x10^5) were washed twice and incubated alone or mixed with mitomycin-C-treated CTV-1 cells (1x10^6) for 6 hours, or IL-2 (200 IU/ml) for 16 hours at 37°C in 5% v/v CO2. Thereafter, NK cells were selectively enriched from co-culture by CD56 isolation, and RNA was extracted from the samples using the RNAqueousTM Micro Kit (Thermo Fisher Scientific).
!Sample_label_ch1 = Target-probe complex
!Sample_label_protocol_ch1 = Batches of 12 separate samples at one time were prepared as per manufacturer’s instructions.  Platform used was human myeloid innate immunity panel (Catalog number XT-CSO-HMMYLD1-12).
!Sample_hyb_protocol = Samples were hybridized with probes at 65°C for 18 hours before being placed into the automated nCounter™ Prep Station (NanoString Technologies), where samples were affixed to cartridges.
!Sample_scan_protocol = Cartridges were immediately placed into the nCounter™ Digital Analyzer (Nanostring Technologies) and read at maximum resolution
!Sample_description = Control
!Sample_data_processing = Using nSolver software, QC  was carried out using default QC parameter settings. Then, raw data files  were examined to ensure that counts of positive and negative controls as well as housekeeping/endogenous genes meet expectations. Thereafter, background noise was adjusted by background thresholding using a user-defined threshold count value of 20 counts. Normalization was accomplished using the geometric mean of the positive control counts, and housekeeping genes in the CodeSet Content. Differential expression was calculated by specifying NK alone samples as the baseline of the experiment using nSolver software.

!Sample_submission_date = Apr 15 2019
!Sample_last_update_date = Jun 11 2019
!Sample_type = RNA
!Sample_channel_count = 1
!Sample_source_name_ch1 = Tumor-primed NK cells (6h)
!Sample_organism_ch1 = Homo sapiens
!Sample_taxid_ch1 = 9606
!Sample_characteristics_ch1 = tissue: peripheral blood
!Sample_characteristics_ch1 = cell type: natural killer cells
!Sample_treatment_protocol_ch1 = NK cell stimulation was achieved by co-incubating CD56+ NK cells (1x10^6) with CTV-1 (2x10^6) for 6 or 16 hours, or the exogenous cytokine IL-2 (200IU/ml) for  16 hours at 37ºC, 5% v/v CO2 in CM.
!Sample_growth_protocol_ch1 = NK cells were isolated from healthy donor PBMCs by positive selection for CD56 (CD56 MicroBeads; Miltenyi Biotec) according to the manufacturer’s instructions. Freshly isolated NK cells were maintained in complete medium (CM) (RPMI 1640 supplemented with 10% v/v fetal bovine serum and 2mM L-glutamine; all from Life Technologies). The  acute lymphoblastic leukemia cell line CTV-1 was maintained in CM.
!Sample_molecule_ch1 = polyA RNA
!Sample_extract_protocol_ch1 = To prepare the samples, resting NK cells (5x10^5) were washed twice and incubated alone or mixed with mitomycin-C-treated CTV-1 cells (1x10^6) for 6 hours, or IL-2 (200 IU/ml) for 16 hours at 37°C in 5% v/v CO2. Thereafter, NK cells were selectively enriched from co-culture by CD56 isolation, and RNA was extracted from the samples using the RNAqueousTM Micro Kit (Thermo Fisher Scientific).
!Sample_label_ch1 = Target-probe complex
!Sample_label_protocol_ch1 = Batches of 12 separate samples at one time were prepared as per manufacturer’s instructions.  Platform used was human myeloid innate immunity panel (Catalog number XT-CSO-HMMYLD1-12).
!Sample_hyb_protocol = Samples were hybridized with probes at 65°C for 18 hours before being placed into the automated nCounter™ Prep Station (NanoString Technologies), where samples were affixed to cartridges.
!Sample_scan_protocol = Cartridges were immediately placed into the nCounter™ Digital Analyzer (Nanostring Technologies) and read at maximum resolution
!Sample_description = Tumor-primed NK cells (6h)
!Sample_data_processing = Using nSolver software, QC  was carried out using default QC parameter settings. Then, raw data files  were examined to ensure that counts of positive and negative controls as well as housekeeping/endogenous genes meet expectations. Thereafter, background noise was adjusted by background thresholding using a user-defined threshold count value of 20 counts. Normalization was accomplished using the geometric mean of the positive control counts, and housekeeping genes in the CodeSet Content. Differential expression was calculated by specifying NK alone samples as the baseline of the experiment using nSolver software.

!Sample_type = RNA
!Sample_channel_count = 1
!Sample_source_name_ch1 = Tumor-primed NK cells (6h)
!Sample_organism_ch1 = Homo sapiens
!Sample_taxid_ch1 = 9606
!Sample_characteristics_ch1 = tissue: peripheral blood
!Sample_characteristics_ch1 = cell type: natural killer cells
!Sample_treatment_protocol_ch1 = NK cell stimulation was achieved by co-incubating CD56+ NK cells (1x10^6) with CTV-1 (2x10^6) for 6 or 16 hours, or the exogenous cytokine IL-2 (200IU/ml) for  16 hours at 37ºC, 5% v/v CO2 in CM.
!Sample_growth_protocol_ch1 = NK cells were isolated from healthy donor PBMCs by positive selection for CD56 (CD56 MicroBeads; Miltenyi Biotec) according to the manufacturer’s instructions. Freshly isolated NK cells were maintained in complete medium (CM) (RPMI 1640 supplemented with 10% v/v fetal bovine serum and 2mM L-glutamine; all from Life Technologies). The  acute lymphoblastic leukemia cell line CTV-1 was maintained in CM.
!Sample_molecule_ch1 = polyA RNA
!Sample_extract_protocol_ch1 = To prepare the samples, resting NK cells (5x10^5) were washed twice and incubated alone or mixed with mitomycin-C-treated CTV-1 cells (1x10^6) for 6 hours, or IL-2 (200 IU/ml) for 16 hours at 37°C in 5% v/v CO2. Thereafter, NK cells were selectively enriched from co-culture by CD56 isolation, and RNA was extracted from the samples using the RNAqueousTM Micro Kit (Thermo Fisher Scientific).
!Sample_label_ch1 = Target-probe complex
!Sample_label_protocol_ch1 = Batches of 12 separate samples at one time were prepared as per manufacturer’s instructions.  Platform used was human myeloid innate immunity panel (Catalog number XT-CSO-HMMYLD1-12).
!Sample_hyb_protocol = Samples were hybridized with probes at 65°C for 18 hours before being placed into the automated nCounter™ Prep Station (NanoString Technologies), where samples were affixed to cartridges.
!Sample_scan_protocol = Cartridges were immediately placed into the nCounter™ Digital Analyzer (Nanostring Technologies) and read at maximum resolution
!Sample_description = Tumor-primed NK cells (6h)
!Sample_data_processing = Using nSolver software, QC  was carried out using default QC parameter settings. Then, raw data files  were examined to ensure that counts of positive and negative controls as well as housekeeping/endogenous genes meet expectations. Thereafter, background noise was adjusted by background thresholding using a user-defined threshold count value of 20 counts. Normalization was accomplished using the geometric mean of the positive control counts, and housekeeping genes in the CodeSet Content. Differential expression was calculated by specifying NK alone samples as the baseline of the experiment using nSolver software.
!Sample_platform_id = GPL23816

!Sample_title = NK CTV-1 6h donor 3
!Sample_geo_accession = GSM3722272
!Sample_status = Public on Jun 11 2019
!Sample_submission_date = Apr 15 2019
!Sample_last_update_date = Jun 11 2019
!Sample_type = RNA
!Sample_channel_count = 1
!Sample_source_name_ch1 = Tumor-primed NK cells (6h)
!Sample_organism_ch1 = Homo sapiens
!Sample_taxid_ch1 = 9606
!Sample_characteristics_ch1 = tissue: peripheral blood
!Sample_characteristics_ch1 = cell type: natural killer cells
!Sample_treatment_protocol_ch1 = NK cell stimulation was achieved by co-incubating CD56+ NK cells (1x10^6) with CTV-1 (2x10^6) for 6 or 16 hours, or the exogenous cytokine IL-2 (200IU/ml) for  16 hours at 37ºC, 5% v/v CO2 in CM.
!Sample_growth_protocol_ch1 = NK cells were isolated from healthy donor PBMCs by positive selection for CD56 (CD56 MicroBeads; Miltenyi Biotec) according to the manufacturer’s instructions. Freshly isolated NK cells were maintained in complete medium (CM) (RPMI 1640 supplemented with 10% v/v fetal bovine serum and 2mM L-glutamine; all from Life Technologies). The  acute lymphoblastic leukemia cell line CTV-1 was maintained in CM.
!Sample_molecule_ch1 = polyA RNA
!Sample_extract_protocol_ch1 = To prepare the samples, resting NK cells (5x10^5) were washed twice and incubated alone or mixed with mitomycin-C-treated CTV-1 cells (1x10^6) for 6 hours, or IL-2 (200 IU/ml) for 16 hours at 37°C in 5% v/v CO2. Thereafter, NK cells were selectively enriched from co-culture by CD56 isolation, and RNA was extracted from the samples using the RNAqueousTM Micro Kit (Thermo Fisher Scientific).
!Sample_label_ch1 = Target-probe complex
!Sample_label_protocol_ch1 = Batches of 12 separate samples at one time were prepared as per manufacturer’s instructions.  Platform used was human myeloid innate immunity panel (Catalog number XT-CSO-HMMYLD1-12).
!Sample_hyb_protocol = Samples were hybridized with probes at 65°C for 18 hours before being placed into the automated nCounter™ Prep Station (NanoString Technologies), where samples were affixed to cartridges.
!Sample_scan_protocol = Cartridges were immediately placed into the nCounter™ Digital Analyzer (Nanostring Technologies) and read at maximum resolution
!Sample_description = Tumor-primed NK cells (6h)
!Sample_data_processing = Using nSolver software, QC  was carried out using default QC parameter settings. Then, raw data files  were examined to ensure that counts of positive and negative controls as well as housekeeping/endogenous genes meet expectations. Thereafter, background noise was adjusted by background thresholding using a user-defined threshold count value of 20 counts. Normalization was accomplished using the geometric mean of the positive control counts, and housekeeping genes in the CodeSet Content. Differential expression was calculated by specifying NK alone samples as the baseline of the experiment using nSolver software.

^SAMPLE = GSM3722273
!Sample_title = NK CTV-1 16h donor 1
!Sample_geo_accession = GSM3722273
!Sample_status = Public on Jun 11 2019
!Sample_submission_date = Apr 15 2019
!Sample_last_update_date = Jun 11 2019
!Sample_type = RNA
!Sample_channel_count = 1
!Sample_source_name_ch1 = Tumor-primed NK cells (16h)
!Sample_organism_ch1 = Homo sapiens
!Sample_taxid_ch1 = 9606
!Sample_characteristics_ch1 = tissue: peripheral blood
!Sample_characteristics_ch1 = cell type: natural killer cells
!Sample_treatment_protocol_ch1 = NK cell stimulation was achieved by co-incubating CD56+ NK cells (1x10^6) with CTV-1 (2x10^6) for 6 or 16 hours, or the exogenous cytokine IL-2 (200IU/ml) for  16 hours at 37ºC, 5% v/v CO2 in CM.
!Sample_growth_protocol_ch1 = NK cells were isolated from healthy donor PBMCs by positive selection for CD56 (CD56 MicroBeads; Miltenyi Biotec) according to the manufacturer’s instructions. Freshly isolated NK cells were maintained in complete medium (CM) (RPMI 1640 supplemented with 10% v/v fetal bovine serum and 2mM L-glutamine; all from Life Technologies). The  acute lymphoblastic leukemia cell line CTV-1 was maintained in CM.
!Sample_molecule_ch1 = polyA RNA
!Sample_extract_protocol_ch1 = To prepare the samples, resting NK cells (5x10^5) were washed twice and incubated alone or mixed with mitomycin-C-treated CTV-1 cells (1x10^6) for 6 hours, or IL-2 (200 IU/ml) for 16 hours at 37°C in 5% v/v CO2. Thereafter, NK cells were selectively enriched from co-culture by CD56 isolation, and RNA was extracted from the samples using the RNAqueousTM Micro Kit (Thermo Fisher Scientific).
!Sample_label_ch1 = Target-probe complex
!Sample_label_protocol_ch1 = Batches of 12 separate samples at one time were prepared as per manufacturer’s instructions.  Platform used was human myeloid innate immunity panel (Catalog number XT-CSO-HMMYLD1-12).
!Sample_hyb_protocol = Samples were hybridized with probes at 65°C for 18 hours before being placed into the automated nCounter™ Prep Station (NanoString Technologies), where samples were affixed to cartridges.
!Sample_scan_protocol = Cartridges were immediately placed into the nCounter™ Digital Analyzer (Nanostring Technologies) and read at maximum resolution
!Sample_description = Tumor-primed NK cells (16h)
!Sample_data_processing = Using nSolver software, QC  was carried out using default QC parameter settings. Then, raw data files  were examined to ensure that counts of positive and negative controls as well as housekeeping/endogenous genes meet expectations. Thereafter, background noise was adjusted by background thresholding using a user-defined threshold count value of 20 counts. Normalization was accomplished using the geometric mean of the positive control counts, and housekeeping genes in the CodeSet Content. Differential expression was calculated by specifying NK alone samples as the baseline of the experiment using nSolver software.

^SAMPLE = GSM3722274
!Sample_title = NK CTV-1 16h donor 2
!Sample_geo_accession = GSM3722274
!Sample_status = Public on Jun 11 2019
!Sample_submission_date = Apr 15 2019
!Sample_last_update_date = Jun 11 2019
!Sample_type = RNA
!Sample_channel_count = 1
!Sample_source_name_ch1 = Tumor-primed NK cells (16h)
!Sample_organism_ch1 = Homo sapiens
!Sample_taxid_ch1 = 9606
!Sample_characteristics_ch1 = tissue: peripheral blood
!Sample_characteristics_ch1 = cell type: natural killer cells
!Sample_treatment_protocol_ch1 = NK cell stimulation was achieved by co-incubating CD56+ NK cells (1x10^6) with CTV-1 (2x10^6) for 6 or 16 hours, or the exogenous cytokine IL-2 (200IU/ml) for  16 hours at 37ºC, 5% v/v CO2 in CM.
!Sample_growth_protocol_ch1 = NK cells were isolated from healthy donor PBMCs by positive selection for CD56 (CD56 MicroBeads; Miltenyi Biotec) according to the manufacturer’s instructions. Freshly isolated NK cells were maintained in complete medium (CM) (RPMI 1640 supplemented with 10% v/v fetal bovine serum and 2mM L-glutamine; all from Life Technologies). The  acute lymphoblastic leukemia cell line CTV-1 was maintained in CM.
!Sample_molecule_ch1 = polyA RNA
!Sample_extract_protocol_ch1 = To prepare the samples, resting NK cells (5x10^5) were washed twice and incubated alone or mixed with mitomycin-C-treated CTV-1 cells (1x10^6) for 6 hours, or IL-2 (200 IU/ml) for 16 hours at 37°C in 5% v/v CO2. Thereafter, NK cells were selectively enriched from co-culture by CD56 isolation, and RNA was extracted from the samples using the RNAqueousTM Micro Kit (Thermo Fisher Scientific).
!Sample_label_ch1 = Target-probe complex
!Sample_label_protocol_ch1 = Batches of 12 separate samples at one time were prepared as per manufacturer’s instructions.  Platform used was human myeloid innate immunity panel (Catalog number XT-CSO-HMMYLD1-12).
!Sample_hyb_protocol = Samples were hybridized with probes at 65°C for 18 hours before being placed into the automated nCounter™ Prep Station (NanoString Technologies), where samples were affixed to cartridges.
!Sample_scan_protocol = Cartridges were immediately placed into the nCounter™ Digital Analyzer (Nanostring Technologies) and read at maximum resolution
!Sample_description = Tumor-primed NK cells (16h)
!Sample_data_processing = Using nSolver software, QC  was carried out using default QC parameter settings. Then, raw data files  were examined to ensure that counts of positive and negative controls as well as housekeeping/endogenous genes meet expectations. Thereafter, background noise was adjusted by background thresholding using a user-defined threshold count value of 20 counts. Normalization was accomplished using the geometric mean of the positive control counts, and housekeeping genes in the CodeSet Content. Differential expression was calculated by specifying NK alone samples as the baseline of the experiment using nSolver software.

^SAMPLE = GSM3722275
!Sample_title = NK CTV-1 16h donor 3
!Sample_geo_accession = GSM3722275
!Sample_status = Public on Jun 11 2019
!Sample_submission_date = Apr 15 2019
!Sample_last_update_date = Jun 11 2019
!Sample_type = RNA
!Sample_channel_count = 1
!Sample_source_name_ch1 = Tumor-primed NK cells (16h)
!Sample_organism_ch1 = Homo sapiens
!Sample_taxid_ch1 = 9606
!Sample_characteristics_ch1 = tissue: peripheral blood
!Sample_characteristics_ch1 = cell type: natural killer cells
!Sample_treatment_protocol_ch1 = NK cell stimulation was achieved by co-incubating CD56+ NK cells (1x10^6) with CTV-1 (2x10^6) for 6 or 16 hours, or the exogenous cytokine IL-2 (200IU/ml) for  16 hours at 37ºC, 5% v/v CO2 in CM.
!Sample_growth_protocol_ch1 = NK cells were isolated from healthy donor PBMCs by positive selection for CD56 (CD56 MicroBeads; Miltenyi Biotec) according to the manufacturer’s instructions. Freshly isolated NK cells were maintained in complete medium (CM) (RPMI 1640 supplemented with 10% v/v fetal bovine serum and 2mM L-glutamine; all from Life Technologies). The  acute lymphoblastic leukemia cell line CTV-1 was maintained in CM.
!Sample_molecule_ch1 = polyA RNA
!Sample_extract_protocol_ch1 = To prepare the samples, resting NK cells (5x10^5) were washed twice and incubated alone or mixed with mitomycin-C-treated CTV-1 cells (1x10^6) for 6 hours, or IL-2 (200 IU/ml) for 16 hours at 37°C in 5% v/v CO2. Thereafter, NK cells were selectively enriched from co-culture by CD56 isolation, and RNA was extracted from the samples using the RNAqueousTM Micro Kit (Thermo Fisher Scientific).
!Sample_label_ch1 = Target-probe complex
!Sample_label_protocol_ch1 = Batches of 12 separate samples at one time were prepared as per manufacturer’s instructions.  Platform used was human myeloid innate immunity panel (Catalog number XT-CSO-HMMYLD1-12).
!Sample_hyb_protocol = Samples were hybridized with probes at 65°C for 18 hours before being placed into the automated nCounter™ Prep Station (NanoString Technologies), where samples were affixed to cartridges.
!Sample_scan_protocol = Cartridges were immediately placed into the nCounter™ Digital Analyzer (Nanostring Technologies) and read at maximum resolution
!Sample_description = Tumor-primed NK cells (16h)
!Sample_data_processing = Using nSolver software, QC  was carried out using default QC parameter settings. Then, raw data files  were examined to ensure that counts of positive and negative controls as well as housekeeping/endogenous genes meet expectations. Thereafter, background noise was adjusted by background thresholding using a user-defined threshold count value of 20 counts. Normalization was accomplished using the geometric mean of the positive control counts, and housekeeping genes in the CodeSet Content. Differential expression was calculated by specifying NK alone samples as the baseline of the experiment using nSolver software.

^SAMPLE = GSM3722276
!Sample_title = NK IL2 donor 1
!Sample_geo_accession = GSM3722276
!Sample_status = Public on Jun 11 2019
!Sample_submission_date = Apr 15 2019
!Sample_last_update_date = Jun 11 2019
!Sample_type = RNA
!Sample_channel_count = 1
!Sample_source_name_ch1 = Lymphokine-activated NK cells
!Sample_organism_ch1 = Homo sapiens
!Sample_taxid_ch1 = 9606
!Sample_characteristics_ch1 = tissue: peripheral blood
!Sample_characteristics_ch1 = cell type: natural killer cells
!Sample_treatment_protocol_ch1 = NK cell stimulation was achieved by co-incubating CD56+ NK cells (1x10^6) with CTV-1 (2x10^6) for 6 or 16 hours, or the exogenous cytokine IL-2 (200IU/ml) for  16 hours at 37ºC, 5% v/v CO2 in CM.
!Sample_growth_protocol_ch1 = NK cells were isolated from healthy donor PBMCs by positive selection for CD56 (CD56 MicroBeads; Miltenyi Biotec) according to the manufacturer’s instructions. Freshly isolated NK cells were maintained in complete medium (CM) (RPMI 1640 supplemented with 10% v/v fetal bovine serum and 2mM L-glutamine; all from Life Technologies). The  acute lymphoblastic leukemia cell line CTV-1 was maintained in CM.
!Sample_molecule_ch1 = polyA RNA
!Sample_extract_protocol_ch1 = To prepare the samples, resting NK cells (5x10^5) were washed twice and incubated alone or mixed with mitomycin-C-treated CTV-1 cells (1x10^6) for 6 hours, or IL-2 (200 IU/ml) for 16 hours at 37°C in 5% v/v CO2. Thereafter, NK cells were selectively enriched from co-culture by CD56 isolation, and RNA was extracted from the samples using the RNAqueousTM Micro Kit (Thermo Fisher Scientific).
!Sample_label_ch1 = Target-probe complex
!Sample_label_protocol_ch1 = Batches of 12 separate samples at one time were prepared as per manufacturer’s instructions.  Platform used was human myeloid innate immunity panel (Catalog number XT-CSO-HMMYLD1-12).
!Sample_hyb_protocol = Samples were hybridized with probes at 65°C for 18 hours before being placed into the automated nCounter™ Prep Station (NanoString Technologies), where samples were affixed to cartridges.
!Sample_scan_protocol = Cartridges were immediately placed into the nCounter™ Digital Analyzer (Nanostring Technologies) and read at maximum resolution
!Sample_description = Lymphokine-activated NK cells
!Sample_data_processing = Using nSolver software, QC  was carried out using default QC parameter settings. Then, raw data files  were examined to ensure that counts of positive and negative controls as well as housekeeping/endogenous genes meet expectations. Thereafter, background noise was adjusted by background thresholding using a user-defined threshold count value of 20 counts. Normalization was accomplished using the geometric mean of the positive control counts, and housekeeping genes in the CodeSet Content. Differential expression was calculated by specifying NK alone samples as the baseline of the experiment using nSolver software.

!Sample_title = NK IL2 donor 2
!Sample_geo_accession = GSM3722277
!Sample_status = Public on Jun 11 2019
!Sample_submission_date = Apr 15 2019
!Sample_last_update_date = Jun 11 2019
!Sample_type = RNA
!Sample_channel_count = 1
!Sample_source_name_ch1 = Lymphokine-activated NK cells
!Sample_organism_ch1 = Homo sapiens
!Sample_taxid_ch1 = 9606
!Sample_characteristics_ch1 = tissue: peripheral blood
!Sample_characteristics_ch1 = cell type: natural killer cells
!Sample_treatment_protocol_ch1 = NK cell stimulation was achieved by co-incubating CD56+ NK cells (1x10^6) with CTV-1 (2x10^6) for 6 or 16 hours, or the exogenous cytokine IL-2 (200IU/ml) for  16 hours at 37ºC, 5% v/v CO2 in CM.
!Sample_growth_protocol_ch1 = NK cells were isolated from healthy donor PBMCs by positive selection for CD56 (CD56 MicroBeads; Miltenyi Biotec) according to the manufacturer’s instructions. Freshly isolated NK cells were maintained in complete medium (CM) (RPMI 1640 supplemented with 10% v/v fetal bovine serum and 2mM L-glutamine; all from Life Technologies). The  acute lymphoblastic leukemia cell line CTV-1 was maintained in CM.
!Sample_molecule_ch1 = polyA RNA
!Sample_extract_protocol_ch1 = To prepare the samples, resting NK cells (5x10^5) were washed twice and incubated alone or mixed with mitomycin-C-treated CTV-1 cells (1x10^6) for 6 hours, or IL-2 (200 IU/ml) for 16 hours at 37°C in 5% v/v CO2. Thereafter, NK cells were selectively enriched from co-culture by CD56 isolation, and RNA was extracted from the samples using the RNAqueousTM Micro Kit (Thermo Fisher Scientific).
!Sample_label_ch1 = Target-probe complex
!Sample_label_protocol_ch1 = Batches of 12 separate samples at one time were prepared as per manufacturer’s instructions.  Platform used was human myeloid innate immunity panel (Catalog number XT-CSO-HMMYLD1-12).
!Sample_hyb_protocol = Samples were hybridized with probes at 65°C for 18 hours before being placed into the automated nCounter™ Prep Station (NanoString Technologies), where samples were affixed to cartridges.
!Sample_scan_protocol = Cartridges were immediately placed into the nCounter™ Digital Analyzer (Nanostring Technologies) and read at maximum resolution
!Sample_description = Lymphokine-activated NK cells
!Sample_data_processing = Using nSolver software, QC  was carried out using default QC parameter settings. Then, raw data files  were examined to ensure that counts of positive and negative controls as well as housekeeping/endogenous genes meet expectations. Thereafter, background noise was adjusted by background thresholding using a user-defined threshold count value of 20 counts. Normalization was accomplished using the geometric mean of the positive control counts, and housekeeping genes in the CodeSet Content. Differential expression was calculated by specifying NK alone samples as the baseline of the experiment using nSolver software.

!Sample_title = NK IL2 donor 3
!Sample_geo_accession = GSM3722278
!Sample_status = Public on Jun 11 2019
!Sample_submission_date = Apr 15 2019
!Sample_last_update_date = Jun 11 2019
!Sample_type = RNA
!Sample_channel_count = 1
!Sample_source_name_ch1 = Lymphokine-activated NK cells
!Sample_organism_ch1 = Homo sapiens
!Sample_taxid_ch1 = 9606
!Sample_characteristics_ch1 = tissue: peripheral blood
!Sample_characteristics_ch1 = cell type: natural killer cells
!Sample_treatment_protocol_ch1 = NK cell stimulation was achieved by co-incubating CD56+ NK cells (1x10^6) with CTV-1 (2x10^6) for 6 or 16 hours, or the exogenous cytokine IL-2 (200IU/ml) for  16 hours at 37ºC, 5% v/v CO2 in CM.
!Sample_growth_protocol_ch1 = NK cells were isolated from healthy donor PBMCs by positive selection for CD56 (CD56 MicroBeads; Miltenyi Biotec) according to the manufacturer’s instructions. Freshly isolated NK cells were maintained in complete medium (CM) (RPMI 1640 supplemented with 10% v/v fetal bovine serum and 2mM L-glutamine; all from Life Technologies). The  acute lymphoblastic leukemia cell line CTV-1 was maintained in CM.
!Sample_molecule_ch1 = polyA RNA
!Sample_extract_protocol_ch1 = To prepare the samples, resting NK cells (5x10^5) were washed twice and incubated alone or mixed with mitomycin-C-treated CTV-1 cells (1x10^6) for 6 hours, or IL-2 (200 IU/ml) for 16 hours at 37°C in 5% v/v CO2. Thereafter, NK cells were selectively enriched from co-culture by CD56 isolation, and RNA was extracted from the samples using the RNAqueousTM Micro Kit (Thermo Fisher Scientific).
!Sample_label_ch1 = Target-probe complex
!Sample_label_protocol_ch1 = Batches of 12 separate samples at one time were prepared as per manufacturer’s instructions.  Platform used was human myeloid innate immunity panel (Catalog number XT-CSO-HMMYLD1-12).
!Sample_hyb_protocol = Samples were hybridized with probes at 65°C for 18 hours before being placed into the automated nCounter™ Prep Station (NanoString Technologies), where samples were affixed to cartridges.
!Sample_scan_protocol = Cartridges were immediately placed into the nCounter™ Digital Analyzer (Nanostring Technologies) and read at maximum resolution
!Sample_description = Lymphokine-activated NK cells
!Sample_data_processing = Using nSolver software, QC  was carried out using default QC parameter settings. Then, raw data files  were examined to ensure that counts of positive and negative controls as well as housekeeping/endogenous genes meet expectations. Thereafter, background noise was adjusted by background thresholding using a user-defined threshold count value of 20 counts. Normalization was accomplished using the geometric mean of the positive control counts, and housekeeping genes in the CodeSet Content. Differential expression was calculated by specifying NK alone samples as the baseline of the experiment using nSolver software.
